# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="9bfec-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-104">El elemento **ResponseCode** proporciona información de estado sobre la solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="9bfec-1479">Comentarios</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-1479">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-1480">Este elemento no es obligatorio y no se incluye en todas las respuestas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-1480">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="9bfec-1481">El esquema que describe este elemento se encuentra en el directorio virtual IIS que hospeda los servicios Web Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9bfec-1481">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
